<gmapID>0x80dd33759e801657:0xd8ca42ee372b95d5<//gmapID>< Text>
In 2016 I was rear ended by a young driver who was texting while driving downhill and collided with me at full speed while I was stopped at a red light. When I got home that evening after going to the Urgent Care for an exam, I knew that I needed to find a good lawyer in my area. I was very happy to find Catherine has an office conveniently near my home. Her practice is with her partner and husband Dan McGee, and it is among the highest rated in reviews in the entire area. Google five stars is certainly well deserved.

I felt very strongly that by them having an office nearby meant that I would essentially be better served. This was in fact the case because when I called it was well after normal business hours and Catherine not only took my call, but listened to my entire story and offered to take my case. She provided me immediate counsel with a suggested plan for my medical treatment and a legal case. I felt sure right away that I would be okay and that I would receive proper medical care and fair, sincere representation in making a claim with the responsible party's insurance company.

Given the fact that I had severe whiplash and other significant injuries, my recovery plan required months of chiropractic care and treatment, at a doctor that I selected, and I have recovered since the treatment has ended. My car was badly damaged but was repaired by a highly rated local shop of my choosing that used original manufacturer parts and gave a generous 1 year warranty on all parts and labor of the entire repair.

The responsible party's well-known large insurance company felt that my case was not significant and did not want to settle my claim. So Catherine asked Dan McGee to arrange for a deposition on my behalf, which he attended with me. He then arranged for the responsible party's deposition as he had fled to Texas to avoid the case. He was found, served the proper paperwork, and deposed. His insurance company convinced him to move back to L.A. and to be available for the proceeding and settlement of this case. As it turned out this case went to an actual courtroom trial, and Dan was absolutely superb in his conduct, presentation, and professionalism. The Jury deliberated for a short while and voted entirely in our favor, thus returning a verdict in the case to my satisfaction.

Catherine, Dan, and their entire team proved to me that I found the best legal representation when I made the call and selected their office in this case. I of course had many questions both large and small that came up through the process. They took the time to explain things in a clear and gentle manner that gave me the best understating of the issue and detail at hand, even on the weekend on a Sunday!!!  it was absolutely superb!

I am sincerely pleased with the level of their caring and experienced service and thankful that they took pride and genuine professionalism in their work. This influenced a very positive feeling throughout my case and certainly gave me a lot of peace of mind. I highly encourage you to call them, you will be treated with well qualified consideration, and care.<//Text>

< Review>
5.0 star rating 2/14/2017
McGee Lerer & Associates was an absolute great pleasure to work with. I was T-boned in a hit an run accident in 2016. After the accident my insurance company offered me the bare minimun for my injuries and the physical therapy I would need to heal. This is when I knew I needed someone to guide me, so I went looking for help.

I found Catherine through google and read about her experience in representing people who had been inolved in accidents. After reading the great reviews I decided to give her a call, we met at her Long Beach office. I told her what happened and she gave me the answers I was looking for. That day I knew she was the right person to handle my case. As I went to physical therapy and finding a new car among other things, Catherine and her assistant Kelly took care of everything legal, so I could focus on my job, college and getting better. When Catherine found that I had a small amount of coverages she advised me to up my insurance in case of any other accidents.

I did and boy am I happy I listened because only 3 and a half months later I was in another accident where I was not driving and was rushed to the hospital were I called her to inform her I was in another accident and would be in the hospital for over a week. If Catherine had not advised me to up my insurance I would've been in a deep hole financially because the person that was driving had the least amount of insurance. Because Catherine I had up'd my insurance. My underinsured motorist insurance is why I was fully compensated for my injuries in both accidents. McGee Lerer are not just a law group but have become extended family, They took great care of me and I will forever be grateful to Catherine, Kelly and the rest of the team...<//Review>

Chill. Well laid out. They do seem to offer backorders.< /review>
<Pictures>None</Pictures><Resp>{'time': 1622404086468, 'text': 'Thanks for the great 5 star review.  Hope you visit us again.'}<//Resp><gmapID>0x80db1ba45681c907:0x887750dd969aa4< /gmapID></record></dataset><record>
< text>
I have known Stephen socially for years and was thrilled when I heard that he was turning his passion into his business. I live in NYC and read DC occasionally and have a place that I like to go to browse and pick up new and back issues (I am currently collecting old Little Archies). Unfortunately, due to the pandemic laws, the shop was not allowed to ship to me nor was I able to go and pickup curbside. So, in April I reached out to Stephen to find out if he'd ship. It seemed ridiculous to buy from a shop all the way on the other side of the country, but I'm glad that I did. Not only could I help a friend, not only could I support a small owner run business, but I appreciated Stephen's passion and work ethic. Let me tell you a brief story - the place I mention above that's here in NYC has a great selection and I really like the guy who runs it, but they fail at followup. I've had to chase them multiple times to order things and simply respond to emails. With Stephen, not only has he been on top of every order/communication, but just a couple weeks ago reached out to me to ask if I'd like to purchase new issues of X&&Z that I have been following. In two days they were in my hand. Now that's a good businessman and anyone who can follow up better than me has my respect and my business. Going forward, as long as it makes sense to continue buying from a store 3000 miles away, I will. BTW the issues showed up in pristine condition. I am truly grateful to Stephen for being able to provide a service during a difficult time. Getting a little package of goodies in the middle of this horror show has been a godsend. I highly recommend Interstellar!!</text>

< review>
Well stocked for new issues from both majors and leading independents but thinly stocked for trades despite acres of shelving of trades. Clean, almost minimalist store display in a modern red/black design scheme.

Friendly and amenable manager. Space has been added at the back for MTG players. Opening hours/days can be unpredictable - best to call the store before making a special trip down there. Good location.

It doesn't have a sense of community yet, but there's a sense that the store is slowly evolving and gradually finding it's way.<//review>

< Text>
Found this place on Yelp for a quite bite and Yelp once again saves the day! I would not have found this place just walking by. It's a bit tough to find and very little seating in here. We came in during happy hour time and a pint of Sapporo was only $3 O_o !! For two of us, we went the route of ordering three little plates and then a ramen bowl to share with the famous hibachi rice that everyone keeps talking about. Sitting at the counter was fun, it went from only 3 of us there and then once we ordered our food, the place was packed with people! As for the ramen, we went with the pork, mild, added an egg and bamboo. All in all, our bill was 35 bucks during happy hour time. Absolutely worth every penny. We tipped the bartender/server very nicely because he was the only one in the place but was attentive. Absolutely will come back again!<//Text>

<review>The hair dryer itself works very well and we are happy with it when it is working. However - ours died 15 months after buying it, and we don't use it everyday. More annoying was their warranty. Although there is a 5-year warranty, you have to pay to ship the broken one back, and pay to have a new one shipped to you. The prices were not very good and it was mostly weird stuff most people do not go to the store to buy, to be quite honest
I bought 3 little salads here, and even the ceaser did not have chicken in it and was 4 dollars. I buy other ones at different stores and they at least have chicken. I love Trader Joe's. I do nearly all my shopping here. They offer a great value on common items but also have many unique foods that your not likely to find anywhere else and all at a great price. Jeffrey Dickman<//Name>
<user_id>112209497970523732050</user_id>< review>
I've been a Trader Joe's customer since my Cal State Fullerton days in the late 1970's. Then there were only a couple off stores. Mine was in Placentia.

Since its early days as a liquor store, which also  carried snacks, evolved into a mid-sized food store carrying unquie products it has developed.

You can easily find enough food to make TJs your main food store. Prices are generally lower than even Stater Bros if such is a factor. They carry plenty of fresh items such as fruits and vegetables including meat, cheese and dairy items.

They carry a large selection of snacks and sweets including an array of nuts, dried fruits, snack chips, cookies and chocolate.

They are, perhaps, best known for its selection of wine and alcohol. Wines are from abroad and domestic, from dry to sweet, white to red, to sangria. Prices range from a few bucks upward. You can always get a nice wine for $10 or less. They also carry various waters, juices, and fresh drinks.

I like the baked goods, which include sourdough, flat breads, multigrain, white and at least two gluten free breads, along with cookies and muffins. Try the corn tortillas at just 99 cents.

Other items of note include vitamins, dog and cat food, flowers, soap, TP, teas and a large selection of frozen foods and snacks.

If you go for one item don't be surprised if you leave with a cart full of food.<//review>
